Britain's Contact with Mediterranean Countries on Mutual Assistance, Several Countries Declare Will Carry Out

Paris: According to the diplomatic correspondent of this agency, it was learned from responsible sources that the British government submitted inquiries to the Mediterranean countries, namely Spain, Turkey, Greece, Yugoslavia, and Romania, at the beginning of this month, stating that if the British Navy is attacked by the Italian Navy in the Mediterranean, can these countries assist Britain at sea? How Spain responded is not yet known here, but it is heard that the governments of the other four countries have all quickly replied, clearly stating that they are prepared to implement the mutual assistance measures contained in Article 16, Section 3 of the League of Nations Covenant. Various technical issues regarding mutual assistance measures will be consulted by experts from the countries concerned in order to supplement the talks previously held between Britain and France on the same issue. (21st Havas Telegram)

Paris: According to news from London, regarding the mutual assistance measures contained in Article 16, Section 3 of the League of Nations Covenant, the British government contacted the Mediterranean countries, asking whether they could assist with strength to cope with future attacks. The spokesperson of the French Ministry of Foreign Affairs neither confirmed nor disavowed this news, but said that the British government had raised questions with France regarding mutual assistance in the Mediterranean, and the French government had replied on October 18 and 26. (20th Havas Telegram)

London: The British government did not consider the replies of the countries satisfactory. When the House of Commons discussed foreign policy yesterday, the cabinet members, led by Eden, stated that the British government failed to obtain sufficient assistance to expand the sanctions policy because of this. Political figures believe that it is more convenient for the League of Nations to preside over the naval mutual assistance negotiations. (20th Reuters Telegram)

London: According to responsible sources, the British government will continue negotiations with the Mediterranean countries so that when the British Navy encounters an attack in the Mediterranean, it can be effectively assisted by these countries. Regarding this level, the British government began negotiations with the governments of Turkey, Greece, Yugoslavia, and Spain on the 8th of this month. The governments of these countries have successively submitted satisfactory replies. As for the purpose of future negotiations, it is to increase the efficiency of mutual assistance methods to resist aggression. As for Romania, although it is not a Mediterranean country, the British government also contacted it because it, Turkey, Greece, and Yugoslavia are all members of the Balkan Entente. (21st Havas Telegram)

Herriot's Christmas Message Wishes Britain, France, and Others Will Cooperate to Create a Better Future for Humanity

London: French Minister without Portfolio Herriot recently sent a letter to the "Tourism and Industrial Association of Great Britain and Ireland" in the form of a Christmas message, saying, "I hope that Britain and France can cooperate closely with other countries to eliminate various misunderstandings between countries and create a better future for humanity." (20th Havas Telegram)

British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain's Speech: Revert to Sanctions Policy, Peace Plan Dead and Cannot Be Resurrected

London: Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain recently delivered a speech in Birmingham, referring to the Anglo-French proposal to resolve the Italian-Ethiopian dispute, saying, "We did make a mistake at one point, which can be admitted. As for this mistake, the point where world opinion was shocked was not realized at the time, but the policy we are pursuing will not change because of this," and said, "The peace plan proposed by Britain and France has now died and has been buried in Geneva. There is no hope of resurrection in the future. I think that all attempts to resolve disputes peacefully have come to an end at this time. Therefore, we must revert to the sanctions policy. If a member state of the League of Nations is attacked because of the implementation of sanctions, I believe that other member states can clearly express that they are ready to jointly assist," and "Therefore, in the next few years, improving national defense to guard against the unexpected is the government's inescapable task." (21st Havas Telegram)

London: The British House of Lords and the House of Commons are resting today until they reopen on February 4. However, they can be convened early if necessary. A railway loan of £26,000,000 to improve railway administration expenses, guaranteed by the government, has been approved by the British Emperor. In addition, several other cases have also been approved. (20th Reuters Telegram)

20,000 Italian Wounded and Sick Soldiers Pass Through Suez

Paris: According to the report released by the Suez Canal Company today, since the outbreak of the war in East Africa, a total of 20,000 Italian sick soldiers have passed through the river and returned home. (20th National Telegram)

Fascist Party Core Cadres Only Express Support for Mussolini, Meeting Still Has No Resolution

Rome: The core cadres of the Fascist Party met at 10:00 PM last night to discuss the Anglo-French peace plan and adjourned at 12:40 AM this morning without any resolution. Another meeting is set for January 18. Although London and other places regard the peace plan as dead, Rome still treats it as surviving. According to a responsible spokesperson, "We have not received a notice that the plan has been canceled." The plan was originally communicated to Rome through diplomatic channels. The Italian government's reply may be issued in the same way, so there is no need to announce it. A press release was issued after the Fascist Party's core cadre meeting, saying that Italy is determined to intensify its resistance to sanctions, and said, "It is now understood that after studying the Paris peace plan in detail on December 18, Britain now considers it invalid."

The core cadres also passed a motion in cheers, declaring the Italian people's unwavering determination to defend their rights and announcing that Italy is determined to continue to move towards the goal of national destiny indicated by Mussolini. A resolution was also passed, announcing that Italian producers are now taking advantage of the opportunities afforded by the current quotas to enable Italy to achieve greater economic self-sufficiency, which can break free from foreign constraints. (21st Reuters Telegram)

Rome: The Fascist Party core cadre meeting continued at the Palazzo Venezia at 10 PM last night, ending at 1:30 AM this morning. A press release was issued afterward, saying, "This meeting discussed the international political situation after the British government abandoned the Laval-Hoare peace plan." It is understood that a motion was passed at the meeting, the general idea being that among the countries implementing sanctions, not only are the opinions mixed, but the phenomenon of going against each other is also more obvious. At this time, the Italian people are still firmly united to defend their due rights. Recently, the people of the country have been of one mind, donating their gold and silver to the country, which is the ironclad proof of the people's determination to resist and win. When this motion was passed, the representatives in the entire stadium cheered loudly. Afterward, it was decided that the soldiers on the front lines and the Blackshirts are the supreme need for Italian civilization, the future of Italy, and the security of Italy. The meeting should send a telegram to them to pay tribute for their hard work in fighting in East Africa. In addition, Volpi, the former Minister of Finance and Chairman of the Italian Industrial Associations, gave a speech, saying that although the sanctions have been implemented for a month, what all agricultural and industrial groups, representing the entire Italian nation, have shown to us is the great spirit of discipline and the firm will to resist. Not only that, Italy can take advantage of this extraordinary situation to promote the development of all domestic production industries, so that it can break away from foreign restraints economically, which is also beneficial to Italy. At this point, the meeting was adjourned until January 18 next year. (21st Havas Telegram)

British Troops in Egypt with Tank Convoy Headed to Libyan Border; Active Defense Preparations Against Italy Underway

Cairo - It was learned today from reliable sources that a British tank convoy secretly headed towards the Italian-Libyan border today. It appears Anglo-Italian relations are becoming increasingly strained. Observers here estimate there are currently 60,000 British naval personnel in Egypt. (20th National Telegram)

Cairo - The destination of the British tank convoy remains a military secret. However, it is rumored that the convoy is heading to the "triangular restricted zone" in northwestern Egypt near Sallum Bay. Since British troops began concentrating on the Libyan border, large numbers of British troops have been transported there. According to reliable sources, there are currently between 85,000 and 120,000 British army and navy personnel in Egypt, as well as 1,000 aircraft, in full wartime deployment. Moreover, according to people arriving from Sallum today, British troops have been actively preparing defenses for several weeks, currently busy digging trenches, installing barbed wire, and concentrating motorized units. Egyptian officials today stated that Egypt will declare its full support for Great Britain. (21st National Telegram)

Changes in British Cabinet; Foreign Secretary Position Temporarily Held by Baldwin

London - There will be changes in the British cabinet personnel during the new year. First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell may retire after the naval conference concludes. It is widely expected that the post of Foreign Secretary will be temporarily held by Prime Minister Baldwin. Some say that Austen Chamberlain is hopeful for the position, but he is known for his association with France, which is currently unpopular, and it is doubtful whether he himself is willing to take on this difficult role. Eden's name is also mentioned frequently, and some still hope for Lord Privy Seal Halifax, but he is already a member of the House of Lords, making it inconvenient for him to accept this position again. Currently, Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain is the most favored. During the House of Commons debate on the Anglo-French peace plan on Thursday, Prime Minister Baldwin's speech was unremarkable. It was Chancellor of the Exchequer's quick thinking and debate with the opposition that saved the cabinet from danger and earned him nationwide praise. Therefore, it is widely believed that he would be able to handle the post of Foreign Secretary competently and happily. The House of Commons has been adjourned until February 4th. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Albanian Army Attacks Italian Outpost; Fierce Fighting in Aksum

Albania - The Albanian army launched a fierce attack on an Italian outpost this morning, and both sides are still engaged in fierce fighting west of the holy city of Aksum. According to official sources, the Albanian army has retaken two Italian defensive positions, along with ten tanks, eighteen machine guns, and two mortars. According to the latest news from Tass, there was hand-to-hand combat for two hours, and Italian aircraft could not assist due to the proximity of the two armies. According to Albanian war news, the Italian army was defeated, with 550 casualties, including 150 Italian officers and soldiers. This Albanian operation clearly aims to carry out its plan to break through the Italian army's right flank west of the holy city of Aksum. (21st Reuters Telegram)

Paris - Former British Foreign Secretary Hoare departed for Switzerland on Sunday and will spend Christmas there, following doctors' orders to rest for three months. This morning, he visited Buckingham Palace to meet with the King. (21st Reuters Telegram)

Albania - The Archbishop issued a message today, ordering the people of Abyssinia to fast and pray for a week, and encouraging the troops on the front lines. (20th National Telegram)

The So-Called Emperor of Abyssinia's Peace Proposal

Paris - The peace plan drafted by the Emperor of Abyssinia before April, which was shelved out of respect for the mediation of European countries for peace, was released here today by the Emperor's foreign advisor, Israel, of the New York People. It states that Abyssinia is willing to cede part of the Tigray province, located between Adowa and Adigrat, to Italy, but excluding Aksum, and exchange a large part of the Ogaden province for Zeila port in British Somaliland or Assab port in Eritrea, and accept the League of Nations' supervision of its administration and diplomacy, but Italy must not enjoy excessive influence. (National Telegram of the Day)

10,000 People Granted Amnesty in Poland Before Christmas to Celebrate the New Constitution

Warsaw - The Senate passed an amnesty bill today to celebrate the new Polish constitution. It is expected that 27,000 people will be freed before Christmas, 60% of whom are currently in prisons throughout Poland, and another 15,000 will have their sentences halved. The Senate also commuted death sentences to long-term imprisonment. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Egyptian King Issues New Election Law; Elections to be Held in May-June of Next Year

Cairo - The King issued an election law today, stipulating that all male citizens of this country who are 21 years of age or older are eligible to vote in the elections for members of the House of Representatives. Criminals and active military personnel are not eligible to vote. To be eligible as a candidate for the House of Representatives, one must be 30 years of age or older, literate, and able to pay a deposit of 150 Egyptian pounds. However, if one fails to obtain one-tenth of the votes in the electoral district, this deposit will not be refunded even if one loses the election. Regarding the qualifications for candidates for the Senate, it is stipulated that they must be 40 years of age or older and possess advanced military, diplomatic, or legal knowledge, or be clergy, or be landowners who pay at least 150 pounds in taxes annually. Administrative officials and members of city councils are not eligible to be candidates for the Senate. In addition, it is stipulated that the list of candidates must be completed before January 31 of next year, but the formal elections will not be held until May or June of next year. (21st Havas Telegram)

US Treasury Advisor Suggests Reopening Silver Conference; Authorities Disagree

Washington - US Treasury advisor Oliphant suggested to the department convening an international silver conference, but the authorities disagreed, because the situation of silver-using countries in the world is unstable, and it is currently not beneficial to convene such a conference. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Washington - According to the report on silver profit tax released today, it can be seen that the profits obtained by American silver merchants in the past 18 months totaled $3 million. The 50% profit tax has abolished the US forward silver market, but has completely eliminated silver speculation. Senator McCarran is reported to be proposing to the next Congress to abolish the tax. (20th National Telegram)

Washington - The Department of Commerce announced today that, according to the first nine months of 1935, Japan's total exports of silver were worth 144,000,000 yen. This is compared to 7,000,000 yen in the same period last year. In September of this year, Japan's silver exports were worth 21,000,000 yen, compared to 1,000,000 yen in the same month last year. Based on what is known about Japan's silver reserves and registered silver imports, it should not be so much. At the same time, the Department of Commerce has received reports of private exports of silver from China being seized. The Department of Commerce also released a report on US-China trade for the first nine months of 1935, stating that US exports totaled $31,667,000, compared to $60,540,000,000 in the same period last year. The Department of Commerce did not criticize the sharp decline in US-China trade but noted that the Chinese authorities believe that China's purchasing power has been reduced due to the US Treasury Department's implementation of the silver purchasing program, which has caused silver prices to rise. (20th Reuters Telegram)

London - In the week ending the 18th of this month, British gold exports decreased significantly, while imports increased. Total exports were £1,536,000, a decrease of £1,036,000 compared to the previous week, of which £1,234,000 was shipped to the United States and £285,000 to France. The total exports for the previous week were £2,572,000. Total imports this week were £4,664,000, of which £68,000 came from France, £2,158,000 from Africa, and £968,000 from China. The total imports for the previous week were £3,146,000. Net imports this week were £2,728,000, compared to net imports of £574,000 last week. (20th Reuters Telegram)

London - In the week ending the 18th of this month, British silver imports and exports both decreased. Total imports this week were £703,000, a decrease of £662,000, of which £678,000 was shipped to the United States, compared to £1,365,000 last week. Total exports this week were £370,000, a decrease of £1,504,000, of which £244,000 came from Japan, compared to £1,874,000 last week. Net exports this week were £333,000, compared to net imports of £509,000 last week. (20th Reuters Telegram)

New York - In the week ending the 13th of this month, the total value of silver imported into the United States was $13,761,000, of which $10,181,000 came from the United Kingdom, $955,000 from Mexico, $1,129,000 from Canada, $696,000 from Hong Kong, and $384,000 from Japan. The total imports for the previous week were $10,251,000, an increase of $3,510,000 this week. (20th Reuters Telegram)

Page 9

Naval Conference Status: Japan Isolated Four Against One; British Shipbuilding Declaration Also Stalled; France to Propose Compromise at Next Meeting

London - Apart from holding a preliminary meeting and a general representatives meeting on December 9th, the Naval Conference has held seven sessions of the First Committee to date. All sessions have been conducted in a friendly atmosphere, focusing on the restriction of naval armaments. The proposals studied so far are: 1) Japan's suggestion to establish a common maximum limit; 2) Britain's suggestion that each country make unilateral and automatic declarations on shipbuilding in the coming years to limit armaments. These two proposals have been thoroughly studied by the public. It is generally agreed that the best way to resolve all issues at the conference is to first review possible solutions, in order to determine the possibility of a fair plan from this analysis. Therefore, judging from the continuous discussions, although the representatives of various countries feel that a qualitative limitation contains great value, a final resolution has not yet been reached on the principles under the alternative methods currently being studied. The committee is scheduled to reconvene on January 6th. (20th Reuters Telegram)

London - The representatives of Great Britain, Japan and the United States have discussed the Japanese and British proposals in the past two weeks, but the views of the three countries' representatives have not changed from the preliminary talks. Although the Japanese representatives have strived to thoroughly implement the principle of disarmament, their effect has only extended to the superficial breaking of the ratio system, and they have failed to completely convince the representatives of various countries. Although the United States and Great Britain have an attitude of respecting the opinions of the Japanese delegation, there is little doubt that the two countries are cooperating to deal with Japan. As for the representatives of France and Italy, due to the subtle relationship of the European political situation, they expressed sympathy to the British government. Regardless of theoretical disputes, the conference situation shows that Japan is isolated with a ratio of four to one. However, the British shipbuilding declaration case has little hope of success due to Japan's strong opposition. A certain US representative expressed pessimistic opinions on this, saying that after the First Committee adjourns, the shipbuilding declaration case is still an issue, but one cannot expect its proceedings to be satisfactory. From this point of view, because the conflicting views of various countries are clear, the meeting enters adjournment, its function is nothing more than temporarily avoiding the crisis of the meeting encountering a deadlock. According to the opinions of the British and other countries' representatives, if the quantitative limitation case cannot be resolved, they want to resolve the qualitative problem. However, the Japanese representatives insisted on the doctrine that quantity and quality cannot be separated, and decided on a policy that absolutely opposes discussing the qualitative limitation case before the quantitative limitation case is resolved. Therefore, after the meeting reopens, it will inevitably fall into a standstill unless a new proposal appears. (22nd Japan United Press Telegram)

London - Advisors to the delegations of various countries to the Naval Conference are currently planning to re-study the British proposal during the Christmas holidays. It is doubtful whether they can find any beneficial points at that time. Judging from the intensity of Japan's opposition to the British proposal during today's meeting of the General Committee, it is also questionable whether this case has any value for continued discussion. Looking at the Naval Conference for the past ten days, no progress has been made. The only result is that the exact nature of the conflicts between the claims and divergent opinions of various countries is becoming increasingly obvious. A certain US representative said, "Although the British proposal has not been abandoned, I have not seen any progress in the discussion." The situation of the Naval Conference can be seen in this statement. (2nd Havas News Agency Telegram)

London - According to what our agency's naval problem reporter knows, the result of today's meeting of the General Committee has sufficiently proved that Japan firmly opposes the quantitative limitation method, even if it wants to maintain the current 5:5:3 ratio in accordance with the plan proposed by Great Britain. When the Naval Conference continues to meet on January 6th of next year, if the common maximum amount system proposed by Japan is not accepted by other countries, and it wants to discuss the issue of qualitative limitation, it is still uncertain whether Japan will accept it. Naval officials predict that if the plans proposed by Great Britain and Japan are not resolved at that time, then the continental countries of Europe, perhaps France, will propose a compromise plan and have it discussed by the Naval Conference. (20th Havas Telegram)

Wuhan Students Hold Parade and Demonstration

20,000 Students from the Three Towns Participate, Maintaining Excellent Order and Issuing Solemn Declaration

Hankou Correspondence: Since the establishment of the Wuhan Middle School and Above Student National Salvation United Association on the 17th, it has authorized the executive committee to actively prepare for a large-scale parade and demonstration. On the 18th and 19th, meetings were held continuously to discuss, elect representatives from each school, and organize a parade committee, divided into six groups: Command Group (Wuhan University), Arrangement Group (Zhonghua University), Document Group (Girls' High School), Propaganda Group (Huazhong University), Discipline Group (Provincial High School), and Transportation Group (Senior Business School). It was decided that the three towns of Wuhan would hold separate parades on the 20th, with Wuhan University and Huazhong University as the general commanders of Wuchang, Zhonghua University and Municipal No. 1 Boys' High School as the general commanders of Hankou, and Higher Engineering School as the general commander of Hanyang. Each school elected a chief leader. Hearing that the government intended to dissuade them, the action was carried out secretly. Late on the 19th, the provincial government received a document from the Student National Salvation United Association and immediately invited members of the provincial and municipal party committees, the mayor of Hankou, and heads of various departments of the provincial government to the provincial government early on the 20th to jointly convene student representatives for talks and dissuasion. The student representatives also stated the purpose of the parade: To awaken the public; To oppose autonomy in North China; To support the patriotic movement in North China; and to solemnly declare that they would maintain order during the parade. The party and government authorities could no longer object, and the students of each school set out separately.

In Wuchang, students from Wuhan University and Huazhong University gathered at the Pingyue Road for a general assembly. More than 10,000 students from over 40 schools, including Huazhong University, Wuhan University, Zhonghua University, Provincial High School, Union Theological Seminary, Bowen, Yujie, Wenxue, Xiangshi, Zhangchu, Wenhua, Provincial Boys' Vocational School, Provincial Girls' Vocational School, Xilida, Chucai, Zhongda Affiliated High School, Girls' Normal School, Experimental School, No. 12 Middle School, No. 9 Middle School, Dajiang, Dagong, Wenhua No. 2, Wuzhong, Art College, College of Education, Huazhong University Affiliated High School, Sanchu, Senior Business School, Provincial No. 1 Girls' Middle School, No. 2 Girls' Middle School, Linghu, and Jingnan, gathered. After the assembly, a command group meeting was held, and Guo Xiyuan, a representative from Wuhan University, was elected as the general commander, with Xu Shengjie from Wuhan University and Zhu Jiayou from Huazhong University as deputy general commanders. The female students were in the front, and the male students were in the rear. The group marched from Pingyue Road through Pinghu Gate to Hanyang Gate. Wuhan University temporarily proposed crossing the river to Hankou to participate. However, Wuhan shipping had been ordered by the Construction Department to suspend service. Unable to fly across the natural barrier, the general and deputy commanders decided that the entire team would be divided into two parts. One part, led by Huazhong University, would march along the original route. The other part, led by Wuhan University, would temporarily stay at Hanyang Gate, and Guo Xiyuan and Zhu Jiayou would go to the Construction Department to request the resumption of ferry service. The request was denied, so they led the team to the provincial government to petition, but it was still difficult to get permission. They stood for a long time. At 3:00 PM, the leaders of each school decided to temporarily leave the provincial government and continue the parade, which proceeded from the assembly at Pingyue Road, through Pinghu Gate, Hanyang Gate, Chayuanpo, Fuyuan Street, Wuchang Road, Yuema Factory, Dachao Street, Baoanmen Main Street, Lanling Street, Zhizimaling, Nanlou, and disbanded at Simenkou. The students who remained at Hanyang Gate were still waiting for the ferry at night, hoping to fulfill their original intention of crossing the river.

In Hankou, the gathering was at Yiyuan. In addition to the full participation of students from various schools in Hankou, each school in Wuchang was notified by the National Salvation Association to send at least 20 students to participate. Students from Wuhan University and several other schools crossed the Han River on the 19th, but many were blocked in Wuchang due to the suspension of ferries and had to cross by private boats. At 10:00 AM, those assembled at Yiyuan included several thousand students from over 20 schools, including Luoyi Girls' High School, Yixun Girls' High School, Zhonghua University, Wuhan University, Xinmian Girls' High School, Jianghan Middle School, Provincial Rural Normal School, Provincial No. 9 Middle School, Municipal No. 1 Boys' Middle School, Aurora Middle School, Wuhan Girls' Middle School, Hanguang Middle School, Wenhua No. 2, E'nan Middle School, Municipal No. 1 Girls' Middle School, Boxue Middle School, Municipal Vocational School, and Hanjiang Middle School. At 11:00 AM, when other students had not arrived, knowing there were obstacles, the parade committee, led by the general commander of Hankou, You Liangguo, a representative from Zhonghua University, and deputy general commanders Yin Jichuan and Zhou Jueshan, ordered the team to set off. Following the planned route, they passed Xinsheng Road to Jianghan Customs, proceeded west along the river, passed the China Merchants Bureau to Minquan Road, turned into Sanmin Road, entered Zhongshan Road, passed Yiyuan again, and entered Special District 3 and Special District 2 to the YMCA, turned onto Huangpi Road, and then along the riverside of Special District 2 to the Lanling Road intersection, where they disbanded.

In Hanyang, the gathering was outside the Higher Engineering School, and the representative from the Higher Engineering School served as the general commander. Students from the Higher Engineering School, No. 12 Middle School, and Yizhi School participated. The Jin Nu Middle School did not participate due to a ban from the school authorities. The route was from the Higher Engineering School through Chang Street to Qingchuan Pavilion, where they disbanded.

In total, over 20,000 students participated in the parades in the three locations. They held banners, shouted slogans, and were full of energy, creating a tense atmosphere. Traffic control and discipline personnel patrolled left and right, so the order was well maintained. The declaration of the Student National Salvation United Association is as follows: "Fellow compatriots, the establishment of our National Salvation United Association stems from a sincere patriotic fervor and fulfills the due duty of citizens. We feel that China's peril has reached a final juncture. If everyone continues to live in a drunken dream, failing to unite and seek salvation, we will witness our beautiful land being completely destroyed. Although we know that many students in Beiping have already sacrificed for the patriotic movement, slaughtered by our own military and police, this is not enough to intimidate us. We have hot blood, we have heads, we have an indomitable spirit, and we have an innate patriotic ambition. Will we still shrink and fear? With the country in imminent danger, we cannot but cry out to the government, cannot but urge the government to make a decision as soon as possible. The violent aggressor is advancing day by day. If we continue to retreat and tolerate, in the near future, our 400 million compatriots will die without a burial place. For the sake of the nation's preservation, for the sake of world peace, and for the sake of justice and righteousness, we will not hesitate to fight to the death. We ask the government to mobilize immediately. Our country is complete and cannot tolerate the existence of so-called autonomous organizations. Yin Rugeng betrays the country, sells territory, and willingly acts as a traitor, which is intolerable to the people of the whole country. We ask the government to issue an immediate order to suppress him and relieve the suffering of compatriots under his rebellious oppression, preserving the integrity of our territory. We ask the government for open diplomacy and the freedom of speech, association, and assembly for the people, which are already enshrined in the law. We ask the government to earnestly protect this. The patriotic movement of students in Beiping is a true expression of popular will. We ask the government to adopt their opinions and ensure their safety, immediately punish the military and police instigators in Beiping, and comfort the dead and injured classmates. The people of the whole country must quickly awaken and unite to safeguard the integrity of the nation's territory and sovereignty and to overthrow our heinous, treacherous, and venomous aggressors." The slogans and banners were as follows: Punish the rebel Yin Rugeng; Forcibly stop all similar autonomous organizations; [Omitted]; We vow to be the backing of our patriotic compatriots in North China; [Omitted]; Please make government diplomacy open; Please mobilize the whole country; The people of the whole country must unite; Please guarantee the patriotic movement; Safeguard the integrity of the nation's territory and sovereignty. (20th)

Han Fuqu Sends Armored Vehicles to Escort Students Back to Their Hometowns; Military and Police Determined to Disperse Student Meetings

Heavy Military and Police Guard at the Gates of All Schools

Jinan Correspondence: Since the students of Jinan High School joined forces with middle schools and other schools in the city to form a National Salvation Corps, Education Director He Siyuan, upon the instruction of Provincial Government Chairman Han Fuqu, issued a notice yesterday (the 18th), ordering all middle schools to suspend classes and go on vacation from the 18th. Military and police were also dispatched to guard the gates of each school. On the 18th, representatives from each school held a plenary meeting to discuss the organization of the National Salvation Corps. After gathering at Zhengyi Middle School, the meeting was dispersed by the military and police before it could even begin. The representatives then gathered at Jinan Rural Normal School and were again expelled. As a result, they gathered at Mount Woniu, more than 20 miles from the city, to hold a meeting. Due to the lateness of the hour, specific measures regarding the organization of the National Salvation Corps were not clearly discussed. On the 19th, students from Jinan Girls' High School, Jinan Girls' Normal School, Jinan Girls' Vocational School, Jinan Normal School, and other schools were forced to leave school by the military and police. Han Fuqu also sent armored vehicles to escort them separately. However, students from Jinan High School, Jinan Middle School, and Private Yuying School did not leave school. The military and police guards at the gates of these schools were even tighter. Students without passes were not allowed to pass, and no one from outside the school was allowed to visit. News reporters were also forbidden from visiting. (19th)

Editor-in-Chief of Hong Kong Kung Sheung Daily News, Lai Kung Chi, Assassinated; Shot in the Abdomen and Leg; Police Detectives Actively Pursuing the Culprit

Hong Kong Correspondence: Lai Kung Chi, the editor-in-chief of the Kung Sheung Daily News, was shot and assassinated by a thug disguised as a coolie on Li Yuen Street East at 1:00 PM on the 16th, after finishing work. Lai was shot twice and fell to the ground. The assassin calmly escaped afterward. The details are listed below:

Details of the Assassination: The entrance of Li Yuen Street East is diagonally opposite the Kung Sheung Daily News. After finishing work at the newspaper office, Lai walked into the street, intending to go straight to Queen's Road. Unexpectedly, when he reached the front of Chang Sheng Hong at No. 1 Li Yuen Street East, he was shot twice from behind by a thug. Lai immediately fell to the ground after being injured. The newspaper office was alarmed by the news, and several staff members rushed to investigate. At that time, Lai had been helped by people from nearby shops to sit on a wooden stool. When he saw his newspaper colleagues, he said, "I was shot twice, once in the abdomen and once in the foot." At that time, an Indian policeman who heard the alarm arrived and called a Red Cross ambulance to the scene to take him to the National Hospital for treatment. Lai was very conscious in the ambulance. His colleagues comforted him, saying that he would be at the hospital soon. Lai was still able to reply, "I know." When the ambulance arrived at the hospital, the doctor happened to be at lunch. Lai urged someone to ask the doctor to come quickly and asked Tan Jia Shi, the doctor, to give him an injection to relieve the pain, saying, "The bullet hit my abdomen." Tan quickly undressed him to examine him but saw no signs and no bleeding. Later, he saw a bluish bruise on his side and examined Lai's back, where he saw two wounds, one entering from behind the right side to the abdomen and one entering from the right thigh. Both bullets were still inside his body. The doctor told him to move his right foot, but Lai replied, "I can't." The doctor then took his pulse and felt that his pulse was very weak, but Lai was still in good spirits at the time, only groaning slightly. Dr. Tan then asked Lai who had shot him and whether he recognized the assassin. Lai replied, "Because the assassin shot from behind, I don't know what the assassin looks like." He then said to the doctor, "Why ask so many questions? Please save me first." The doctor then used a stretcher to carry him to room No. 2, changed his clothes, and prepared for surgery. At that time, Lai was very conscious and said to his colleagues, "There is a key to my desk in my vest pocket. Give it to a colleague to do my work. I don't think I can return to the office tonight." He then said that there were a hundred yuan in his clothes and pants pockets and asked them to give it to his wife. He also asked for paper and pen to write something. Later, feeling unable to support himself, he said to his colleagues that he was very tired and didn't have much hope. He asked them to tell the Kung Sheung Daily News and Southwest Middle School to ask for some money for his mother so that she could return to her hometown and live out her life. At this time, Deputy Superintendent Jia Lude Luo and Detective Assistant Yi Lushi Dun had arrived at the hospital and asked the injured person for a statement as usual. Lai's answers were the same as what he told the doctor. Finally, the detectives asked if he had any enemies he could think of. Although Lai answered, the case was not very clear and could not be published. When the detectives asked Lai the reason again, Lai did not answer because he was tired.

Treatment Process: After the detectives left, the nurses prepared everything for the surgery. When they wanted to use anesthesia, Lai suddenly refused, saying, "This is anesthesia. I don't want to use it," and "I must use an X-ray to see it before cutting." After speaking, he shouted to a colleague outside the ward. However, he was eventually anesthetized by the doctor and carried into the operating room. Before the surgery, according to Dr. Tan Jia Shi, although Mr. Lai was very conscious, his condition was considered extremely serious due to his weak pulse. Now, surgery was the only way to save him. At this time, it was already 4:00 PM. The surgery was then performed by Dr. Tan and several assistants to remove the bullet from his abdomen. It was found that the bullet was a .32 caliber lead bullet. Because the bullet entered from the back of the side, the small and large intestines in the abdomen were pierced. Afterward, the doctor said that although the intestines had been reconnected, the condition was extremely serious because hot blood had flowed back into the abdomen. It was expected that the patient would not be able to sleep tonight (the 16th) and that the wound in the abdomen would become inflamed tomorrow (the 17th). Lai became conscious again around 6:00 PM after the surgery. He ordered his family to come to his bedside and comfort him. Although Lai was very tired at the time, he was still able to say to his family, "Don't cry. I'm fine now. I'm saying these words to comfort you. Go home."

Police Action: After the case occurred, the police immediately took action and went to the scene of the incident on Li Yuen Street East to search pedestrians and inquire about the details from people in nearby shops. Four people who had witnessed the assassin shooting were taken to the police station. It is said that the assassin was about 27 or 28 years old, disguised as a coolie, wearing an old felt hat and carrying a bamboo pole. He followed Lai and used the felt hat to cover the gun when he shot. Afterward, he wrapped the gun in newspaper, put it back in his chest pocket, took a few steps towards Queen's Road, and then slowly walked towards the Central Market after seeing that no one was chasing him. Although the assassin was barefoot, his flesh was very white and he did not look like a coolie. As the police were taking action, Assistant Superintendent Ma Fei went to Lai's mistress's place on Hennessy Road, Wan Chai, to investigate everything. According to Lai's mistress, Lai was shot at by a thug in Sham Shui Po on the 5th. His head was injured, and his felt hat was also pierced. The wound was triangular. Lai chased the thug half a street away but was eventually escaped. Afterward, Lai told his mistress that he had no enemies and that this must have been a case of mistaken identity. Lai's wife, Mrs. Chen, lives on Pokfulam Road. According to her, Lai's head was injured on the 5th because he was hit with the butt of a gun by an enemy. Because the gun suddenly misfired when the thug pointed it at Lai, he angrily used the butt of the gun to injure him. However, according to a relative of Lai, Mr. So-and-so, Lai had received threatening letters a week before being hit on the head with the butt of a gun, expressing extreme dissatisfaction with his duties at a certain newspaper. At that time, his family advised Lai to take strict precautions, but Lai said that he had already published a notice a month ago resigning from his duties at a certain newspaper and did not think he would be hated by anyone. Unexpectedly, this incident happened soon after, which was very unfortunate. After Lai was shot at by a thug in Sham Shui Po and failed, Lai carried his self-defense pistol with him at all times. If the thug had not shot him from behind on the 16th, he would not have escaped so easily.

Lai Kung Chi's Brief History: Lai Kung Chi, from Ningming County, Guangxi, is 44 years old. In his early years, he graduated from the industrial department of Guangxi Second Middle School and the engineering department of the Guangxi Army Military Academy. When Sun Yat-sen opened his government in Guangzhou, he served as an adjutant in the headquarters. When Ma Junwu was the governor of Guangxi Province, he appointed Lai as the magistrate of Longzhou County. He began his career in journalism at the Xiangjiang Morning Post, which was founded by Sun Yat-sen as a revolutionary organ. The Kung Sheung Daily News was founded by Lai and organized to oppose the Communist Party. It has been over ten years since its establishment. He is currently the editor-in-chief of the Kung Sheung Daily News and also served as the supervisor of the Tam Hoi Teng Pao. He was also a teacher at Southwest Middle School in Hong Kong. Last month, he published a notice resigning from his concurrent position at the Tam Hoi Teng Pao. Lai is usually silent and smiles little. He is kind and approachable to others and is good at calligraphy and painting. He devoted himself to the revolutionary cause in his early years. Now, he has been tragically shot by a thug for unknown reasons, which has caused many to sigh. Lai has an elderly mother, wife, and daughter in Hong Kong. His eldest daughter is currently 16 years old, and his son is 11 years old. However, Lai is usually generous, so he has no long possessions at home. His situation is often that of an empty-handed man. The police are now taking this case very seriously and will arrest the culprit and bring him to justice.

Following Luo's Footsteps: Since Hong Kong has had newspapers for 72 years, the incident of a Chinese newspaper reporter being shot by a thug was last year when Luo Weijiang, the president of Tiannan Daily, was shot at by a thug from behind while walking on Longhua Street. Fortunately, Luo immediately ran into a foreign goods store and was able to escape death. Now, Lai Kung Chi has also been shot, making him the second newspaper reporter to be shot in Hong Kong's history. (17th)

Chaoshan Unified Anti-Smuggling; Smuggled Goods Dumping Has Been Sanctioned; Japanese Residents in Shantou Discuss Countermeasures

Shantou Correspondence: Because smuggled goods are rampant in the Chaoshan area, the authorities have implemented unified inspections and divided the Chaoshan area into six inspection zones, all under the jurisdiction of the Chaoshan Land and Water Anti-Smuggling Office. Currently, there are two anti-smuggling platoons in Chaoshan, with 280 soldiers. There are also no fewer than 100 supervisors, special agents, and investigators. In addition, district directors are set up in each county of Chaoyang, Chao'an, Jieyang, Huihe, Raoping Chenghai. Outside the anti-smuggling districts of each county, sub-cards are set up to specialize in the inspection and release of land and water transportation matters. All goods in transit, if there is no special tax certificate attached to the goods or if there is no inspection and release certificate passed by each sub-card, will be considered smuggled goods and punished, confiscated, and the consignor, transporter, and consignee must all be jointly responsible. After this method was implemented, legitimate merchants felt that the procedures were cumbersome, but they believed that following these procedures was tantamount to obtaining protection, and that this method was also a powerful tool to prevent smuggled goods from invading the Chaoshan-Meizhou hinterland and seizing the market, so they were happy to comply. Moreover, the goods of various organized smugglers in Shantou have been piled up like mountains in the bird bridge back warehouses in Shantou since the implementation of this method, making it impossible to transport them to the hinterland. On the 28th of last month, the smugglers sent several sailing ships to dump rice and beans in Chao'an and along the Han River, and two ships were detained under the Xiangzi Bridge. Later, through the intercession of the Republican Foreign Company and a certain foreign rogue, who claimed that the goods were being transported to provide relief to foreign nationals and not for smuggling profits, the anti-smuggling authorities, in order to avoid trouble, agreed to deal with the matter leniently and allowed them to be taken back. Those who usually collude with smugglers have therefore been slightly restrained and dare not continue to transport or sell duty-free smuggled goods on behalf of others. Moreover, legitimate business firms in Chaoshan, after paying taxes on goods transported to the interior according to procedures, are free to buy, sell, and transport through all card ports, so business is beginning to thrive. Because tax-free goods, although cheap, are not as easy to sell as taxed goods, and various grains can be transported in a continuous stream since the unified inspection. The customs is also stepping up anti-smuggling, with the aim of cracking down on the illegal export of silver and the illegal import of goods. Since this month, customs has seized dozens of cases of silver smuggling, worth more than 20,000 yuan, and also seized a large number of smuggled goods on ships and in the city. Yesterday, 66 bags of white sugar and 3 packages of seafood that had been put into the warehouse were seized at the Nanshunfa Commercial Firm on Shangping Road in the city and escorted back to customs. It is reported that the commercial firm is opened by a rogue. Ryuqi Sakamoto, director of the Foreign Affairs Division of the Taiwan Governor-General's Office, arrived in Shantou on the Hai Ning Lun on the morning of the 8th. The Japanese Residents Association, the Taiwan Association, and others immediately convened a meeting to discuss the development of South China's business, the strict anti-smuggling measures in Shantou, and the transportation of goods by trade permits, and made decisions to propose to Sakamoto. This is also a matter that deserves attention.

Anhui Province Repairs River Embankments: Construction Department Plans Outline of Measures

Anqing Dispatch: The Anhui Province river embankment repair project was previously surveyed and estimated in sections by personnel dispatched by the Construction Department. The report was submitted to the National Economic Council, which decided, according to the river closure and embankment restoration clauses, that the central government would bear 342,000 yuan of the construction costs. Subsequently, 500,000 yuan of disaster relief public bonds were reallocated. Currently, the Ministry of Finance and the Central Bank are being contacted via telegram to mortgage the public bonds for cash. According to the National Economic Council's allocation list, the amount borne by the central government for this project is half of the construction costs required for the originally estimated primary projects in Anhui Province. The remaining half must be raised by Anhui Province itself. In addition, essential maintenance and repair projects should also be completed by Anhui Province on its own. Given Anhui Province's current financial resources, it is not easy to raise a large sum of money immediately, so it is planned to utilize civilian labor and make proper overall arrangements. According to the dispatched personnel's survey and estimate, the total amount of earthwork required for the construction of river embankments in Anhui Province is more than 7,060,000 cubic meters. Among them, more than 2,500,000 cubic meters are for closing river breaches, restoring embankments, and building long embankments and new embankments set back from the river. More than 4,500,000 cubic meters are for maintenance and repairs. It is planned to provide a subsidy of 5.5 fen per cubic meter for projects such as closing breaches, and a subsidy of 2.7 fen per cubic meter for maintenance and repair projects. In addition, the project costs that should be borne by the Ma Hua Tongren Embankment and other material costs for closing river breaches and restoring embankments, as well as project management fees, should not exceed the total amount of the originally allocated 342,000 yuan. Regarding construction methods, it is planned to follow the precedent of Anhui Province's repair of the main dikes of the Yangtze and Huai Rivers in the 23rd year of the Republic [1934], with personnel dispatched by the province to supervise and guide the work. The relevant county magistrates will conscript labor and dispatch personnel to assist in the process. Regarding the method of providing subsidies, it is planned to refer to the road repair precedent, with the county magistrates managing the funds. Subsidies will be distributed at any time based on the acceptance certificates made by the supervisors, and the expenses will be reported for verification upon completion of the work. A draft outline of measures for repairing the river embankments has been specially formulated and submitted to the provincial government for review and implementation. The outline of measures is recorded below:

This province has established the Anhui River Embankment Repair Works General Office to oversee and guide the implementation of construction matters. It is attached to the Anhui Province Water Conservancy Engineering Office and has a chief engineer and a deputy engineer, concurrently held by the director of the Water Conservancy Engineering Office and the chief of the Water Conservancy Works Section. Below it are the following works offices and supervisory sections: (Zi) Guanzhuang Embankment Works Office, also supervising the embankments along the Yangtze River in Tongling County; (Chou) Liubai Zhang Embankment Works Office; (Yin) Huangsitan Embankment Works Office, also supervising the embankments along the Yangtze River in Wuwei County; (Mao) Ma Hua Embankment Works Office, also supervising the embankments along the Yangtze River in Susong County; (Chen) Guangji Embankment Works Office, also supervising the embankments along the Yangtze River in Huaining County; (Ji) Wangjiang Supervisory Section; (Wu) Guidong Supervisory Section; (Wei) Fanchang Supervisory Section; (Shen) Wuhu Supervisory Section; (You) Dangtu Supervisory Section; (Xu) Hexian Supervisory Section; (Hai) Tongcheng Supervisory Section. The number of engineering affairs personnel to be dispatched to each of the above works offices and supervisory sections will be determined separately.

The repair of the river embankments shall be carried out according to the dike style stipulated by the National Government's Flood Relief Committee in the 20th year of the Republic [1931], with the dike surface one meter higher than the flood level, the dike surface four meters wide, the outer slope at a ratio of 1:3, and the inner slope at a ratio of 1:2 in the upper part and 1:5 in the lower part.

The repair of the river embankments shall be carried out by the works office or supervisory section, together with the relevant county government, conscripting labor for construction, and designating responsible personnel for each section, referring to the precedent of sectionally supervised repair of the Yangtze and Huai River dikes in this province last year. The work must be completed before the end of April of the 25th year of the Republic [1936]. The rules for conscripting and managing labor will be determined separately.

Each works office and supervisory section shall, based on the actual situation, refer to existing charts and diagrams, strictly adhere to the aforementioned stipulated dike style, set stakes, divide sections, and calculate in detail the amount of earthwork and the number of required laborers. A sectional earthwork and labor calculation table shall be prepared and submitted to the works general office for signature and report to the Construction Department, which will verify and forward it to the provincial government, ordering the relevant county government to conscript civilians according to the plan and have them report to work within a specified time limit. The "Construction Guidelines for Restoring Embankments" issued by the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission shall be followed to supervise and guide the construction. Acceptance inspections shall be carried out at any time, and acceptance certificates shall be issued so that subsidies can be claimed from the county. The detailed rules for the works office and supervisory office will be determined separately.

The aforementioned subsidies shall be calculated on the basis of the National Economic Council's subsidy to this province for river embankment repair, allocating 10% for various project management fees, as well as the amount to be shared between the Ma Hua and Tongren embankments after consultation with Hubei and Jiangxi provinces. The subsidies shall be divided into the following two categories according to the type of project: Category A: Closing breaches, restoring embankments, and constructing or retreating new embankments: (Zi) Guanzhuang Embankment, (Chou) Liubai Zhang, (Yin) Huangsitan, (Mao) Guangji Embankment Baojia Village, (Chen) Mapu Embankment Luhua Pond. Each cubic meter shall be subsidized by 5.5 fen. Category B: All maintenance and repair projects: Each cubic meter shall be subsidized by 2.7 fen.

The branch dikes connecting each section shall be strictly supervised by the relevant county government in accordance with repeated orders from the provincial government to strengthen and repair the valley embankments. Each works office and supervisory section shall also conduct inspections at any time. If there are any deficiencies, a portion of the acceptance certificate for the river embankment section may be deducted.

The river embankment repair subsidies for each county shall be recalculated by the Construction Department of the provincial government based on the original sectional earthwork calculation tables reported by each works office and supervisory section to determine the amount to be given. The funds shall be allocated to the relevant county governments in batches for management. Payments shall be made to workers based on the acceptance certificates issued by the works office or supervisory section, and receipts shall be collected and reported for reimbursement. The detailed rules for each county's management of subsidies will be determined separately. (December 20th)

Fengxian

Land Registration to End Next Summer

Except for the salt fields and wasteland in this county, the land has been completely surveyed by Dong Jinzhao, the director of the Land Bureau, who urged his subordinates to complete the work. Subsequently, registration was carried out based on the surveyed mu division. Landowners from various places, in view of the past chaos in land matters, eagerly hoped for reorganization. Therefore, since the start of registration, they have all enthusiastically registered with their old deeds and recent grain receipts. If there are mortgage relationships, the landowners have also jointly applied for registration with the creditors in accordance with the law. In order to protect creditors' rights and other considerations, the bureau requires landowners who present incomplete or completely lost documents to find a reputable guarantor to bear all responsibilities before registering. Land disputes arising from registration are handled by the bureau's committee at any time. Land that has been registered and has title deeds, as well as land that has not been registered after the deadline, will all be sealed. It is also heard that the person in charge of the bureau said that the overall land consolidation in this county is expected to be completed between May and June next year.

Changzhou

Chamber of Commerce Petitions Ministry of Finance to Amend Silver Management Rules

The Chairman of the Wujin County Chamber of Commerce, Xu Juxi, submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance on the 20th, stating: "According to a letter from the Chairman Jiang Junjia, Standing Committee Member Zhao Huanzi, and Tang Yuzhang of the Gold and Silver Industry Association, it is reported that Article 2 of the 'Silver Management Rules for Silver Products' promulgated by the Ministry of Finance on November 15 stipulates that the manufacture of silver utensils and ornaments should use chemical silver as raw material. If pure silver must be added, the amount of pure silver must not exceed 30%. This concerns the future of our silversmith industry greatly. Silver utensils, vessels, and ornaments have always contained 80% pure silver. If the pure silver content is reduced, the material will be harder and the color will be difficult to keep white. If the material is hard, it will be difficult to shape. If the color is not white, it will not be welcomed by customers. Even if it is successfully shaped, it will be easily broken upon impact. Intricate work such as figures, flowers, and plants will be impossible to make. Moreover, our country's workers are not familiar with science and adhere to traditional techniques. If the original silver content is changed to 30%, it will be extremely difficult for silversmiths to implement. For the sake of the industry's future, we have no choice but to implore your esteemed association to forward this petition to the Ministry of Finance to amend the silver management rules and allow the old silver content to be maintained without restrictions, so as to maintain the business and benefit industry and commerce." Based on this, after investigation, if silver vessels and ornaments contain too little silver, it will not only be difficult to work with but also easily damaged. The various points stated by the industry to preserve its business are truly based on the actual situation. It is appropriate to forward this petition based on the facts, hoping that your ministry will review and approve the modification and continue to handle it according to the old regulations, so as to maintain the business and comply with commercial sentiment.

Shen Baixian Returns from Dongzhuang

Shen, the director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, considered the success or failure of the Dongzhuang Yellow River closure project to be of great importance to the safety of Jiangsu Province. Therefore, he went to investigate in person the other day. Those traveling with him included Xu Kai, the chief engineer of the Huai River Project; Xu Shida, the technical chief of the North China Water Conservancy Commission; Xu Xinwu, the director of the Huai River Project Office of this department; Huang Yan, the section chief of the Shanghai Dredging Bureau; Shi Jiaxi and Zhang Zhongyi, professors of civil engineering at Tsinghua University; and He Zhitai, a professor of hydraulic engineering at Beiyang University. They gathered in Kaifeng on the 14th of this month, arrived at Dongzhuang on the 15th, and inspected the closure worksite for two days before returning to Kaifeng on the 17th and then returning to Zhenjiang. During this trip, he met with Kong Xiangrong, the acting chairman of the Yellow River Commission, to discuss the project in detail. According to Shen, the closure project was originally organized by the Shandong Provincial Government. Since the 16th of this month, it has been transferred to the Yellow River Commission to take over. The original plan was to consolidate the remaining dike of Li Sheng Tun and build it into a solid eastern dike base. It has now been largely completed. Then, a new dike will be connected downstream of the Jiangsu dike to serve as the western dike base, and four water diversion dams will be built to divert the main current into the old river channel. Both are in progress. The acting chairman of the Yellow River Commission, Kong, told him that if there is no significant current during the ice run and the materials are fully prepared, the closure is expected to be completed by March of next year.

At around 4:00 PM on the 18th, a person suddenly came to the Nanhu Hotel and asked Sun how the money issue would be resolved. Seeing the situation was not good, Sun shouted loudly asking what money was being referred to. Hearing the sound, the hotel staff knew that the visitor was not a good person and reported it to the Guanyinge Police Station, which ordered the police to arrest the person. He was taken back for questioning and gave his name as Chen Yanqing, 30 years old, from Xiaoshan, living in Hangzhou, a silk merchant. He admitted to knowing Sun and borrowing money, but denied any previous threats. The arrested bandit was sent to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau. On the 20th, police officer Li questioned him and he confessed to the same facts and was detained for further verification.
