A Visit to the China Pencil Factory (Continued)

— Huang Youxiong

1. The Dawn of Domestic Pencils 2. Pencil Manufacturing Materials 3. Key Points of Pencil Manufacturing 4. Pencil Lead Manufacturing Process 5. Pencil Shaft Manufacturing Process 6. Machinery and Equipment 7. Other Products 8. Brief History of the China Pencil Factory

(5) Pencil Shaft Manufacturing Process

The wood used is linden wood, which has already been cut into strips of the appropriate size. Each piece of wood makes up half of a pencil shaft, with grooves cut into both pieces to accommodate the pencil lead. When joined together, they form five pencil shafts. However, this work is not easy, as the initial wood is not very dry and needs to be dried in a drying machine for four to five hours. It is then bundled tightly to prevent warping and unevenness. After being stored in this way for a month, it is sent to a core groove manufacturing machine to create fine grooves. These grooves must be very precise, neither too wide nor too narrow. Once the grooves are in place, the pencil lead is inserted, glue is applied, and the two pieces are joined together. They are then tightly bound and further dried before being planed into a round shape and separated into individual pieces.

The shaft boards, made by gluing two pieces together, are first sawn to remove any uneven ends. They are then sent to a planing machine, where one side of the board is planed into five semi-circular shaft rods. The other side is then planed, combining the two semi-circles into a circular shape, and individual round pencils fall from the planing machine. At this point, they are pencils, but they have not yet been finished or made aesthetically pleasing. Finishing involves polishing the round shape and then applying paint. Polishing is easy, but painting requires at least seven coats, and sometimes up to twenty. The pigments used must also be finely ground beforehand. After painting, a lacquer is applied to give a glossy finish. The ends are then cut off to improve appearance. Finally, the manufacturer's name and brand are stamped on with lead foil, and they are packaged for sale in the marketplace.

(6) Machinery and Equipment

A small pencil goes through such a complicated manufacturing process. Readers will surely find this unexpected. However, despite the complexity, it does not feel strenuous because all the work is done by machines. As long as the electricity is well-managed, it is not difficult. Not only is grinding and pounding done by mechanical power, but the removal of wood shavings from the planing machine and the oiling and air supply for the lead core furnace are all done with automatic devices. Painting is done by machine, printing is done by machine. Everywhere, there are machines. People only need to manage the machines, so what difficulty is there? As a result, although the China Pencil Factory is not large in scale, its daily output can currently reach 50 to 100 baskets, and at most, it can produce 200 to 300 baskets. Its brands currently used are "Airplane" and "Ding." Within the "Airplane" brand, there are also "Little Friend," "Good Student," "Student National Products Year," and "Aviation Room Save the Nation," etc. There is no need to introduce these in detail here.

(7) Other Products

The above description refers specifically to ordinary black lead pencils. At the same time, the China Pencil Factory also manufactures various high-grade pencils. The difference between colored pencils and ordinary pencils is that the former does not use lead but instead uses a glue-based color. The clay used must be extremely fine and is often ground for seven to ten days. After adding the pigment, it is steamed for a day and then rolled. The rest of the process is the same as for making ordinary pencils.

(8) Brief History of the China Pencil Factory - The China Pencil Factory was initiated in the winter of 1933 and preparations began in July 1934. The capital was 50,000 yuan. At that time, the directors of preparation were Mr. Yang and Mr. Mei Zhangweishi. Mr. Wu graduated from Yokohama Higher Technical School in Japan with a degree in applied chemistry and had interned for over a year at the Masaki Yamato Pencil Company in Japan. Therefore, he possessed rich knowledge and experience in this industry. Although the preparation period was extremely rushed, by March of this year, the various machines had been installed one after another. Workers were trained and raw materials were purchased. By the end of June, products were being produced. Because they were entirely domestic goods, they were well-received by society. The factory officially opened on November 8 of this year. From now on, it is hoped that its products will become increasingly refined and its production will increase daily to supply the people of the country and to plug the leaks of the nation. (End)

Shen Garden Basketball Court Sold Out - Lianghua Defeats McLaughlin by a Large Margin - Score 57-33 - Li Zhenzhong's Wonderful Shots Widely Appreciated

The Lianghua basketball team came to Shanghai, and in their first game last night, they defeated the McLaughlins by a large margin, 57-33. Li Zhenzhong's wonderful shooting earned him much praise. The team's teamwork was excellent, and their coordination was skilled. They are expected to perform even better against the Pirates. Good basketball games have been scarce in Shanghai recently, so last night, nearly 2,000 people went to Shen Garden to watch the game. The large Shen Garden basketball court was temporarily declared sold out. Lianghua's appeal is evident.

Lianghua's Style Remains the Same - This year's McLaughlins team is much weaker than in previous years. They ranked very low in the YMCA league, so Lianghua's victory was expected. Their defense was weak, and their shooting was poor. They relied solely on Xiang Sheng's individual effort. Lianghua's style was as elegant as ever. Li Zhenzhong's shooting was most appreciated. Liu Zhenyuan seemed to have improved, while Tang Baokun seemed ordinary. The two defenders were exceptionally solid, and Zhang Jingshi was even more impressive. However, the excessive number of fouls last night was a flaw. During attacks, their passing was often too complicated, often resulting in mishaps and missed opportunities.

Tense Situation at the Beginning - After the start, the McLaughlins took the offensive. Xiang Sheng scored under the basket, opening the scoring. Liu Zhenyuan responded with a basket, tying the score. With Pierre's shot, the McLaughlins took the lead again. Li Zhenzhong and Zhang Liangshi scored in succession, but the McLaughlins did not show any weakness. The two teams exchanged points, with the score fluctuating by one point. Lianghua struggled to find a way through. With Griffin's score, the McLaughlins took a 16-14 lead. Fortunately, Li Zhenzhong scored repeatedly, and Lianghua took the lead again, 18-16. The tension of the situation was evident.

Lianghua's Turning Point - The McLaughlins tried to use their tall stature to make things difficult for Lianghua, but it was difficult to succeed. At this time, Huiaide was suddenly substituted for Griffin to play center. From then on, Lianghua found a turning point and soared to new heights. Li Zhenzhong, Zhang Jingshi, and Liu Zhenyuan worked together to increase the score continuously. The McLaughlins remained the same, only scoring one point from a free throw. The result of the first half was 29-17, with Lianghua leading by twelve points.

McLaughlin Collapses - After the Lemon Time, Lianghua exerted its power even more, achieving success with ease. McLaughlin collapsed and could not cope, with the score reaching 50-27, a difference of twenty-three points. Zhang Jingshi and Yin Hongxiang, the two defenders, were both ejected for four fouls, but this could not shake the overall situation. The final result was 57-33, a great victory for Lianghua.

Municipal Stadium No. 1: Report on Yesterday's Industry and Commerce Football Match

There were three matches yesterday afternoon at the Municipal Stadium No. 1 Industry and Commerce Football Association. The first was between Youheng and Municipal Earthworks of the German group. The skill level of the two teams was about the same, but due to the strong wind and wet ground, the players found it difficult to display their skills. Therefore, the first half was a back-and-forth affair with no progress. In the second half, Youheng's center forward took a long shot from 35 yards out, which surprisingly hit the mark, causing a loud cheer. In an instant, they broke through the defense again from a corner kick opportunity, creating a 2-0 lead. Youheng won. In the second match, Yingguang played Shudong of the Angle group. Within minutes, Yingguang scored from a free kick long shot. The Shudong goalkeeper was careless and missed the save. In the second half, after switching sides, Yingguang had the advantage of the wind, and their momentum increased. First, the right inside forward charged out diagonally and scored a goal. Then, the left inside forward scored two consecutive goals in the thick of the action, making it 4-0. Thus, the light of Yingguang surpassed the dawn of Shudong. In the third match, Takahashi played Double Ten of the ball group. Overall, the game was extremely intense. The individual skills and teamwork of both sides were quite impressive. The official battle resulted in each team scoring one goal within five minutes. The speed of passing and the skill of shooting were equally matched. Subsequently, the battle intensified, with the attackers exhausting their ability to charge and break through, and the defenders creating deep trenches and high barriers. Ultimately, the strength was equal, and neither side could achieve anything. Until the middle of the second half, when the Double Ten rear guard was resisting the enemy's chaos, Takahashi's center forward flew in alone, breaking through the encirclement. The Double Ten goalkeeper was caught off guard and was ultimately defeated. Thus, the tie was broken, and Takahashi won with a score of 2-1.

Education News

Ministry of Education Orders the Allocation of Disaster and Illness Reserve Funds for Overseas Students

(Nanjing, 21st) The Ministry of Education has instructed various departments to investigate the fact that provinces and cities should allocate reserve funds for government-funded overseas students and store them in the overseas student management agencies in the countries where the students are studying, to be used for unexpected events such as disaster relief and medical treatment. The Ministry's regulations for studying abroad already stipulate this. Recently, the Overseas Student Supervision Office in Japan reported that some provinces and cities have still failed to comply, making it impossible for the office to deal with urgent educational needs of government-funded students on a temporary basis. Please issue a general order requiring the education departments of all provinces and cities with government-funded students to quickly establish reserve funds. The establishment of these reserve funds is indeed necessary. Provinces and cities that have already sent government-funded students should find ways to allocate reserve funds to the overseas student management agencies in the countries where the students are studying to meet emergency needs. Those that have not yet sent government-funded students should also pay special attention to this when sending government-funded students. This order must be complied with.

Ministry of Education Issues Circular to Draft Management Measures for Free Education Funds

(Nanjing, 21st) In order to carefully manage and audit the expenditure of free education funds in various provinces and cities, the Ministry of Education issued a circular to all education departments on the 21st, requiring them to draft management measures for free education funds and submit them to the Ministry for review within one week of receiving the document.

National Language Speech Competition of East China Universities: Guanghua Wins Team Championship

Second Place, Hujiang; Third Place, Jinnan; All Received Awards Regularly. First Place Individuals: Gu Cunjie, Tan Weihan, Hu Ti. English Speech Competition Today at 2:00 PM at Jiaotong University.

The National Language Speech Competition of East China Universities was held yesterday afternoon starting at 2:00 PM in the Wen Zhi Hall of Jiaotong University. Eighteen contestants from nine schools participated. It concluded at 6:00 PM. Guanghua University won the team championship. Gu Cunjie, Tan Weihan, and Hu Ti shared first place individually. The English speech competition will be held again at Jiaotong University this afternoon at 2:00 PM. Details are as follows:

Representative Meeting: At 9:00 AM, a meeting of representatives from each school was held. Li Kuandu and Li Qingtan of Jinnan, Hu Zhining of Guanghua, Pi Songnian and Hu Jingming of Fudan, Zhou Huaijiu and Huang Chengzhu of the Business School, Pei Gongsen of Jinling, Zhu Yueshan and Zhu Meixian of Jinling Women's University, Yang Xunzheng and Ji Ruixing of Jiaotong University, and Sha Rongcun and Yang Chenglu of Hujiang attended. Yang Xunzheng chaired the meeting, and Zhu Meixian recorded the minutes. The various prizes were distributed, and Chen Heying, Zhu Shaoping, and Gui Zhongshu were hired as judges for the English speech competition.

Contestants: This year, nine schools participated in the National Language Speech Competition, with two representatives from each school. They included Ai Guoyan and Zuo Songyin from National Central University, Yin Guoying and Tan Weihan from Guanghua, Cheng William and Liu Jingfeng from Jiaotong University, Xiong Zhenqi and Gu Cunjie from Hujiang, Zhu Meixian and Liu Peijin from Jinling Women's University, Shen Yiwei and Hu Ti from Jinnan, Li Qi and Chen Chaohan from Fudan, Huai Qiqiang and Hua Shishu from the Business School, and Zhu Peinong and Feng Qijing from Jinling University. There were four female students and the rest were male. Tan Weihan of Guanghua, Zhu Meixian of Jinling Women's University, and Cheng William of Jiaotong University were all representatives who had won prizes in the previous competition.

Competition Begins at 2:00 PM: The competition started at 2:00 PM. Chairman Li Zhaohuan (replaced by Chen Jiaxun), judges Pan Gongzhan, Wu Yaxing (replaced by Chen Gaoyong), and Wang Yunwu (replaced by Wei Pengdan) arrived, along with more than 300 students and audience members. The chairman first reported the competition standards, which were divided into four items: thought, structure, posture, and tone, each accounting for 25%. Prizes were awarded to the top five individuals and the top three teams. Each person's speech time was ten minutes. The timekeeper rang the bell at eight minutes as a warning. Audience members were not allowed to applaud and were not allowed to enter or leave the venue while the speech was in progress. Then, according to the pre-drawn order, the speeches began.

Competition Results: The competition ended at around 5:00 PM. The judges determined the rankings. The team awards were: first place, Guanghua University; second place, Hujiang University; third place, Jinnan University. The individual rankings were: first place, Gu Cunjie of Hujiang, topic "Do It"; also first place, Tan Weihan of Guanghua, topic "Children Should Have a Children's Year"; also first place, Hu Ti of Jinnan, topic "The Theory and Practicality of Land Collective Ownership"; second place, Qiu Guoying of Guanghua, topic "Understanding Our Era"; third place, Xiong Zhenqi of Hujiang, topic "The Road to Self-Improvement"; fourth place, Zhu Meixian of Jinling Women's University, topic "The National Character That China Needs"; fifth place, Zhu Peinong of Jinling University, topic "From the Economic Crisis to Monetary Reform". Then, judge Wei Pengdan awarded the prizes on the spot.

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society Begins on the 26th of This Month

The Chinese Economic Society is an organization founded by Chinese economists. It was established in 1923 and has a history of twelve years. It currently has more than 600 members. The society usually holds its annual meeting in July or August. Last year's annual meeting was held in Changsha. This year's 12th annual meeting is scheduled to be held from the 26th to the 29th of this month at the Guangzhou Hotel. Members from Shanghai have been traveling to Guangzhou one after another and are scheduled to return to Shanghai on the Haiyuan Wheel on January 1 of next year. Details are as follows:

Attending Members: More than a dozen members from Shanghai, including the president of the society, Liu Dajun, and other members, have already traveled to Guangdong on the China Merchants Bureau's Haiheng Wheel. More are continuing to travel to Guangzhou. Including members from Guangzhou, approximately 50 members are expected to attend this year's annual meeting. Most are bankers and economists who enjoy the Ministry of Railways' preferential treatment for academic national members. The China Merchants Bureau also offered discounts on transportation.

Meeting Schedule: The meeting schedule for this year's annual meeting has been set as follows: Day 1, December 26 (Thursday): Opening at 9:00 AM: 1. Opening ceremony, 2. Chairman's speech, 3. Guest speeches, 4. Paying respects at Huanghuagang. Lunch hosted by President Zou of National Sun Yat-sen University, followed by a visit to the new campus of Sun Yat-sen University. In the afternoon, discussion of papers. Dinner hosted by Chairman Lin of the Provincial Government and Commander-in-Chief Chen, followed by a tour of Guangzhou City. Day 2, December 27 (Friday): Discussion of papers in the morning. Lunch hosted by the Guangdong Economic Design Commission. In the afternoon, visit to the new sugar factory. Dinner hosted by Mayor Liu of Guangzhou City, followed by a tour of the Pearl River. Day 3, December 28 (Saturday): Discussion of papers in the morning. Lunch hosted by President Zhong of Lingnan University. In the afternoon, visit to the Xicun Cement Factory and various chemical industrial manufacturing plants in Xicun. The society affairs meeting will be held in the evening. Day 4, December 29 (Sunday): Full-day visit to various agencies and organizations, and a trip to Huangpodong or Conghua Hot Springs. Lunch hosted by the Guangzhou Chamber of Commerce. Dinner hosted by the society to thank all sectors of Guangzhou.

Preparatory Committee: The members of the preparatory committee for this year's annual meeting have also been appointed as follows: A. Paper Group: Li Zhaohuan, Wang Yunwu, Tang Fengzeng, Li Quanshi, Li Bojia. B. Hospitality Group: Hu Jixian, Ling Ji, Huang Yuanbin, Huang Yinpu, (Guangzhou) Li Yunliang, Wang Zhixin, (Shanghai) Zhou Yichun, He Lian, (Tianjin) Xu Qingfu, (Hangzhou) He Haoruo, (Changsha) Jia Shiyi, Dong Xiujia, (Wuhan) Chen Changheng, Zhang Sichuan, (Nanjing) C. General Affairs Group: Liu Dajun, Wu Xiaoyuan.

Conference Papers: The scope of this year's conference papers is "The Economic Policies That China Should Adopt in the Future," which is also the central issue for discussion regarding China's economy. Many members have submitted papers. Those that have been printed by the Commercial Press include: Liu Dajun's "China's Economic Control Policies That Should Be Adopted in the Future," Dong Xiujia's "Discussion on China's Highway Policies in the Future," Jia Shiyi's "Rehabilitating Rural Areas Should Implement Agricultural Protection Tariffs," Li Quanshi's "Discussion on China's Tariff Policies," Zhu Tongjiu's "Review of Land Policies and Evaluation of Land Village Ownership," Yao Qingsan's "Several Opinions on the Central Bank," Huang Yuanbin's "Our Country's Exchange Rate Method after Centralized Silver Reserves," Tang Qingzeng's "Observing China's Economic Policies That Should Be Adopted in the Future from a Historical Perspective," and Gu Yiqun's "China's New Monetary Policy and International Economic Equilibrium," etc. There are also other papers that will either be read at the meeting in their original manuscripts or distributed in mimeographed copies due to time constraints.

Commemoration of Yu Huaiqing by the Huatong Public School

The late Mr. Yu Huaiqing, the former head of the Chinese Department of the Shanghai Public Concession Bureau's Huatong Public School, taught at the school for 26 years. Many well-known figures in society are his former students. This spring, he passed away due to overwork. He was another fading educational elder in Shanghai. Recently, the school principal and current and former teachers and friends launched a fundraising campaign to commemorate him. Huang Jianxun, Zhou Pinghou, Chen Yuanru, Hu Xianyuan, Chen Baofan, and others were elected to organize the Yu Jun Memorial Fund Raising Committee to collect donations from current and former students in order to realize the following three commemorative measures: Engraving a bronze plaque to be placed in the school; Allocating a portion of the fund, with the annual interest used as a memorial award; Publishing and sending his posthumous work "Spring River Miscellaneous Poems". Many people have been sending donations to Mr. Hu Xianyuan at the school in recent days. Others have been recording the addresses of old alumni and sending them to the school in order to send out letters for solicitation. It can be seen how deeply Mr. Yu's teachings have touched people and that his lifelong dedication to education was not in vain.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (1)(3)(1)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

"Once I had a new pair of shoes, and I wanted to show them off; so, although my mother told me not to leave the garden outside the door, I ran away and wandered around all day. It was in the city, and I don't know how I didn't get run over by a car. I was very proud of myself. At first I played with some dogs in the park, then I played with some strangers and boats in the river, ate some fish and sweet potatoes with a red-haired beggar girl for lunch, and finally, when they found me, I was fast asleep on the doorstep of a house, with my arms around a big dog. It was late at night, and I was as dirty as a little pig, and my new shoes were completely ruined - I had walked too much that day!"

"How interesting!" Nian shouted, looking ready to try it out for himself.

"The next day was not so interesting," Mrs. Shu said, taking care not to let her eyes show how much she still longed for the playfulness of her childhood.

"Did your mother beat you?" Nian asked curiously.

"She only beat me once, and even then she asked me for forgiveness, or else I don't think I would have let it go, because it hurt my feelings too much."

"Why did she ask you for forgiveness? - My father didn't."

"Because after she hit me, I turned around and said, 'Your temper is bad. You deserve to be beaten too.' She looked at me, and suddenly her anger was gone, and she said shamefully, 'You're right, Shu, I was angry; I didn't set a good example for you myself, so how can I punish you for being angry? Forgive me, dear, let's see how we can help each other better.' I never forgot this, and it did me more good than ten beatings."

Commercial News

Finance Gold Price Rises to $1,177 Again Yesterday

Foreign Banks Suffer Losses, Public Anxious and Fearful

Rumors Abound, Rise of $16

Holiday Break for Two Days Starting the 25th

The gold market had previously declined due to a sudden large supply of foreign exchange, but public sentiment turned uncertain. Yesterday, it stabilized initially but then strengthened. Generally, people are concerned about the continuous disastrous fall of foreign banks. In terms of exchange, adjusting funds seems endless, and changes are likely to occur, causing great anxiety. Large investors suddenly reversed from short to long positions, rumors spread, stimulating heavy buying, and the price finally rose to $1,177, a new high since the currency reform. In the morning, overseas silver markets in England and America both fell. The trading floor still said that the United States was buying 8% of the supply. Deferred silver prices in Montreal rose by 1.3 cents and fell by 4.5 cents. Exchange rates were flat. The price of raw gold in London rose by half a penny. Western newspapers reported that the Central Bank shipped a large quantity of silver to the United States last night, worth between $10 million and $16 million, supposedly to stabilize the exchange stabilization fund. The foreign exchange position is expected to be maintained, and public sentiment remains tired. The Central Bank's official rates were announced, with British and American rates unchanged, and the customs gold unit unchanged. The standard gold price was raised to $1,147.60. Off-floor pre-market trading opened, initially bid at $60, but lacked support and fell to $56-57. Dadecheng and Chunyuan Yong took advantage of the low price to buy in, rising to $58-59. After opening, it stabilized initially but then weakened. Citibank and Chase actively sold, causing the price to drop from over $60 to $56. Japanese banks showed good appetite, and buying activity at low prices provided support. HSBC's official rates were announced, with British and American rates unchanged, and public sentiment was extremely uncertain. Although the price rose to above the $60 mark, due to the erratic supply of large investors, it lingered around $60 for quite some time. The announcement of a silver equalization tax reduction of 2.5 cents had little impact. Later, rumors of the Central Bank opening cash again stimulated buying and caused the price to rise, but it still lingered. Afterwards, public sentiment became actively optimistic. Various favorable rumors circulated on the floor, and the price broke through the $70 mark again. At this point, some selling occurred as large investors took profits, causing a temporary decline. However, buyers kept coming, so suppliers gave in, and another round of price increases began, rising to $277. However, the trend was weaker after the noon session, and there was a decline. The total number of contracts increased to over 13,200, with the long side outnumbering the short side by 25. Future prospects are inevitably subject to change. Here is a record of the market situation for half a day:

The morning opening was at $1,158.30. Fuxing Yong and Dadecheng Huixiang bought in, rising to $60.20. Hengyu Yifeng Yong sold at high prices, falling to $58.50. Dada Fuxing Yong Shang took delivery, rising to $59. Hengyu Xianghe Huixiang Fuxing Yong sold contracts one after another, falling to $56. Fuyu Fuxing Yong, although rising to $57.10, soon fell back to $56 due to selling from Richang. Dadecheng Hengyu Yuqing Yong Fuxing Yong took delivery of contracts at low prices, rising to $58.80. Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

### A Christmas Gift

— Shouqiu

Dear children, the annual celebration of Jesus's birth, Christmas, has arrived once again! I know that on Christmas night, you will all be expecting gifts from Santa Claus. But that is impossible. Because Santa Claus will never come to your houses! Therefore, you will surely be disappointed in the end.

However, dear children, you don't need to lose heart. Now, I will represent Santa Claus and give you a very precious gift. What is this gift? It is the two words, "Diligence" and "Frugality." If a person can be diligent in their studies and diligent in their work, then their future will surely be very promising. As for the word "Frugality," it refers to thriftiness. A person who is thrifty will be content with prices and will not have thoughts of plunder, or corruption! Therefore, the ancients had the saying, "Frugality cultivates integrity."

Diligence and frugality are the foundations of wealth and honor. Wealth comes from frugality, and honor comes from diligence. Therefore, a family that is diligent and frugal will be prosperous, and a country that is diligent and frugal will be wealthy. However, the habits of diligence and frugality are cultivated from childhood, so I hope that you children will also cultivate the habits of diligence and frugality from a young age.

Donate New Year's Money to Relief Efforts

— Shafei

How quickly time flies! Only a few pages remain of the calendar for the 24th year. Yes, that old foreign trickster who specializes in swindling our money is active in the market again. Children! You all know that this scene means that the new 25th year is coming soon.

The annual old custom of sending New Year's cards is about to begin again at this year's end. Children! Perhaps these days you are busy spending a lot of time and money on New Year's cards. True, this is a courtesy, but we must think carefully about whether we can afford to congratulate each other in these times?

At the same time, we must think about this: we are eating our fill and staying warm. But what about the suffering compatriots in the disaster areas? They are hungry and cold, waiting to be fed and rescued! Of course, we children should also fulfill our obligations. Let's save the money for sending New Year's cards and donate it to disaster relief! This, I think, is what all the children are willing to do, right?

Plant Life in Winter

— Zhen

The weather is gradually getting colder, and the leaves on the trees are falling one by one. As a result, Min'er has added a lot of clothes. One day, he was thinking, "It's getting cold, and we're all wearing thick clothes. But the leaves on the trees are falling one by one. Aren't they cold?"

"Brother, why do trees lose their leaves in winter? What's the reason for this?"

"When deciduous trees enter winter, they don't get enough sunlight and moisture, so the leaves gradually turn yellow and fall off one by one. As a result, the machinery for making food is gone. Transpiration and assimilation also stop, and the roots completely stop absorbing water, so life is cut off and it becomes a dormant state. This situation is probably because the amount of sunlight and heat decreases in winter. The chlorophyll in the leaves no longer absorbs carbon dioxide from the air. On the one hand, because moisture decreases, the absorption function of the roots also weakens and cannot replenish water, so transpiration stops to prevent the branches and trunk from drying out. On the other hand, the life cycle of leaves is also limited. After the limit is passed, they cannot survive, so at this time, a separation layer forms at the base of the petiole. There is a ring around the outside of the separation layer. The cells inside this separation layer die, so after the wind blows, the leaves fall off."

"Brother, then why don't some trees lose their leaves in winter? What's the reason for this?"

"These trees that don't lose their leaves are called evergreens. They can withstand the cold in winter, and even if the sunlight is not strong, they can still grow, so they still develop as usual, but they grow more slowly than in warm weather. However, their leaves don't stay on the tree forever either. They also fall off after a certain period of time, but on the one hand, the leaves are falling off, and on the other hand, new leaves are also growing, so it feels like the leaves are green and won't wither all year round."

Worth Introducing Children's Toys

— Baling

Everyone knows that children's nature is very curious and active, so toys are really their only gift. Every child's favorite toy is as important as their favorite snack. Unfortunately, in recent years, the import of foreign toys has been increasing, causing a large amount of our Chinese money to flow abroad to purchase children's toys. According to customs statistics, the import of foreign toys in one year last year reached a huge six million yuan. Just ask, is this not an alarming statistic? Is this not a frightening number? If we don't find a way to remedy this, then the outflow of money will really be a very terrible crisis.

Now it's good, our Chinese domestic factories also have self-made domestic toys coming out. The factory that created children's toys is the well-known Kangyuan Can Factory, which implements scientific management methods. As far as I know, they have already produced plush toys, including elephants, dogs, horses, monkeys, crocodiles, frogs... and more than a dozen others. Each toy has a mechanism inside, so when the mechanism is activated, it can move like a real animal, which is very attractive. And the price is very cheap, so ordinary families can afford to buy them.

As Student Domestic Product Year is about to end, I sincerely recommend these domestic active toys to all the dear and lovely children, hoping that you children will buy more domestic toys from now on, fulfill your responsibility to promote domestic products for the country, so that you can be worthy of the country, be worthy of society, and at the same time, be worthy of yourselves?

Keep Hands and Feet Clean

— Peiyu

Experience tells us that cleanliness is a very effective way to protect the body and prevent disease. Our body must be clean, and our hands and feet must also be clean. Because there are many bacteria and microbes that specialize in transmitting various diseases and destroying human health. These things are so small that our naked eyes cannot see them, but they can be seen clearly under a microscope. They are most afraid of cleanliness, so we must use cleanliness to defeat them and eliminate them.

First, we must develop a simple healthy habit, which is to clean our hands and feet. We must wash our hands with soap and clean water before eating and after using the toilet. It is even better to wash with medicated soap. Fingers, palms, backs of hands, and wrists must be washed clean, especially the fingernails; because in this small area, there can be hidden millions of bacteria, microbes, and other dirty things. Fingernails must not only be cleaned at all times, but also be trimmed often to prevent these harmful disease-causing things from hiding inside.

Our feet should be washed once every night before going to bed. A little salt can be added to the water for washing the feet. In summer, the temperature should be lower than our body temperature. We should pay attention to our toenails as we do to our fingernails, and trim them at least once a week. Be careful when trimming them, and don't cut off too much. It is best to keep the toenails level with the tips of the toes. Cutting off too much can easily cause the toenails to embed in the flesh. Even if they don't embed in the flesh, the tips of the toes will hurt when they come into contact with shoes and socks. As for the socks worn, it is best to use wool or cashmere. Socks made of cotton or silk and cotton blends are not very suitable, because these socks lack elasticity and hinder the development of the feet.

Fishing Diary

— Written by Mi Wenhuan

This is a real bird. Oh no! It fell into the fish's mouth. I'll catch it. Great! Great! Only some bones left? No bird meat to eat, but there's fish meat to eat.

The Words of a Violin

— Yueqi

My name is Violin,

I am the queen of the orchestra, the most brilliant of the "string" aristocracy. Sometimes I sing the highest note, but sometimes I also act as an assistant. In string music, there are more "firsts" than "seconds." This is different from human life.

My family boasts that I was born from the silver bow of the "God of Archery" Apollo, but others whisper that the seven-string lyre is one of my ancestors! Regardless, I am very faithful: I express whatever emotions people give me.

I first became prominent in Italy. The time was in the 17th century, when opera needed a "highest note lyre" to accompany the high notes. Soon someone discovered that my tone was so beautiful that great music that imitates the human voice could not be complete without me. My wood was carefully selected and kiln-dried; my strings were elegantly arranged; the finest varnish was used to make my body shine; at that time, I was truly never happier.

Thus, in the hands of a musician, I can express all kinds of emotions - mercury-like fluid and continuous melodies, intermittent dance music, vibrating tremolos, gorgeous finger-tapping sounds, heart-pounding vibrato, weeping glissandos, soft harmonies, and other impressions given to people.

However, in order for the human expression to reach the highest level, I must have a beautiful bow. Yes, I pay special attention to my bow, just like a beautiful little girl pays special attention to her beautiful clothes.

A Three-Dimensional New Year's Card

— Dong Xun

One year passes and another comes, the old year passes, and the Chinese Republic's twenty-fifth New Year is coming again soon! Of course, your friends have sent you New Year's cards, and you can't help but send them back. But if you go to the store to buy New Year's cards, the cheap ones are not beautiful, and the beautiful ones are very expensive. Now I will tell you how to make a three-dimensional New Year's card. It doesn't take much time, and the cost is very low. The style is both beautiful and very novel. If you send it to your friends, they will definitely be very welcome!

Manufacturing method:

First, take a sheet of drawing paper and cut it into two pieces, "one" and "two," according to Figure A (the size can be determined according to the ratio). Punch a small hole in "one" and cut a chimney "three" and insert it into the hole. Then glue "one" and "two" together. "One" can be left uncolored. Color the walls of "two" in yellow or blue, the door in a lighter shade of yellow or blue, and the window in white or cut it out and paste a transparent thin paper on the back, like a small glass window.

Cut a rectangle from thick and hard drawing paper, and then cut and fold "four" according to Figure E and glue B onto it. In addition, take three or four thorny cypress branches, insert them next to the house, two on each side, as shown in Figure E. The lower part of the cypress branches must be long (as shown in Figure C) so that they can be inserted into the drawing paper (as shown in Figure D).

After the special project is done to the part of Figure E, another piece of thick and hard drawing paper must be prepared, with the upper part colored in azure or light blue - white is also acceptable. Write the words "Happy New Year, Wishing You Progress... So-and-so respectfully congratulates you. So-and-so bows..." in red in advance, and then paste E on it, as shown in Figure G; at this time, most of the project is completed, and only a very important part remains, which is "snowing." The so-called "snowing" is to scrape the chalk into fine white powder with a small knife, and then apply glue (not too thick) to the top of the house, on top of the small trees, and on the ground, and then sprinkle the chalk powder on it to make it stick, so that the snowflakes fall on the house, trees, and ground. However, the glue must be applied evenly, otherwise if it is applied drop by drop, the chalk will be glued into lumps! After making the large paper sheet G, cut a frame according to Figure F with another thick and hard paper sheet and glue it on it to support it so that it can stand on a desk or other things. That way: the work is completed!

After the three-dimensional New Year's card is made, if you want to send it by mail, then you need to prepare a three-dimensional box separately, otherwise you can send it yourself.

Finally, I also want to tell you children a few words, that is, the method I have described is just a very simple one. I hope that you children can use it as an inspiration to create more beautiful and more complex ones! At the same time, I hope to make an animated New Year's card for you next year!

The Tale of the Righteous Dog (II)

— Xinqing

The two of them were very poor - extremely poor, often going many days without anything to eat. They really did not have the chance to eat their fill, and when they were able to eat comfortably, it would feel like entering Heaven. However, the old man was very gentle and kind to the child, and the child was pure and honest, and gentle by nature; they were happy when they got a few breadcrumbs or some vegetable leaves, and they had nothing else to ask of the world. In truth, as long as Patrasche was with them, bearing the hardships together, they would be satisfied; if they did not have Patrasche, they would not know what to do.

Because Patrasche was their whole life; their treasure and granary; their gold mine and source of wealth; their Secretary of State and breadwinner; their only comfort and good friend. If Patrasche died or left them, then they would have to lie down and die together. Patrasche was the two of them, grandfather and grandson, their hands and feet; their body and mind; in short, Patrasche was their life, which was their soul.

Because old Daas was too old, and a disabled person; Nello was a small child, but Patrasche was their loyal and strong dog.

It was a Flanders dog - yellow fur, a big head and limbs, wolf-like erect ears, legs and feet very strong, clearly honed from many years of hard labor.

Patrasche's parents were both dogs accustomed to hard work. For a lifetime, they went back and forth on the uneven roads of Flanders, doing the hard and tiring work. When Patrasche was born, he inherited from his parents the idea of only doing hard work for humans. He suffered enough abuse and endured enough beatings, and he could only endure everything. Why? Because it was still a Christian country, and he was just a dog.

From the time it was born, it had not yet grown, and it first tasted the bitterness of leather collars and wooden carts, pulling carts all day long for people to travel. Before it was even thirteen months old, it became the private property of a metal merchant, who routinely ran from south to north; from the green sea to the green mountains. Because it was too small, it was sold cheaply to this merchant.

This merchant was a drunkard and a villain. Patrasche lived in hell every day. Its master was wicked and never cared about its life or death. He often filled his cart with many metal bottles and cans, and made Patrasche pull them desperately, while he swayed his fat body and strolled lazily to the side, smoking his black pipe, stopping to eat and drink at every hotel or coffee shop along the way.

But Patrasche, whether fortunate or unfortunate, was eventually a strong dog, because it was born of an iron-strong race, and could withstand all kinds of tyrannical treatment; so it did not die, but struggled to prolong its painful life under the constant beating, abuse, hunger and thirst.
